The direct formula He\texorpdfstring{$^\wedge$}{\string^}\{(m)\}\+\_\+n = n!/\+(n-\/m)!\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\+He\+\_\+\{n-\/m\}(x) (where He\+\_\+j(x) is the j-\/th probabilists\textquotesingle{} Hermite polynomial and He\texorpdfstring{$^\wedge$}{\string^}\{(m)\}\+\_\+j(x) its m-\/th derivative) is employed. \Hypertarget{namespace_c_a_p_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_s_p_a97304bd6170e48a0ceae2f9a51e285c5}\index{CAP::MATH::SP@{CAP::MATH::SP}!hermite\_prob\_series@{hermite\_prob\_series}}
